  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0) then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in (195.87.177.128/27) then
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

end-policy

route-policy IKSV_IMPORT
  delete community all
  if destination in (62.244.235.8/32, 84.44.78.192/28) then
    set local-preference 100
    set weight 0
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy IPv6-BGP-LU
  if destination in PFX-ALL-BGP-IPv6-LU-LOOPBACKS then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy Mete_deneme
end-policy
!
route-policy TURKNET_xxxx
  #REJECT BOGONS_V6
  if destination in BOGONS_V6 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/48
  if destination in Smaller_than_48 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_LONG_AS_PATH
  if as-path length ge 50 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT DEFAULT
  if destination in ipv6_def then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT OLD IPT/PNI COMM 
  if community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT IPT COMM
  if community matches-any IPT_COMM then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT PNI COMM
  if community matches-any PNI_COMM then
    drop
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ###########################################
  #MOBILE FULL
  if as-path in ASN_MOBILE then
    done
  endif
  #FIX FULL
  if as-path in ASN_FIX then
    done
  endif
  #LOCAL FULL
  if as-path in ASN_LOCAL then
    done
  endif
  #CUSTOMERS 
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    done
  endif
  ################################  EXCEPTIONS_END  ###########################################
  #REJECT OTHERS
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy netflix-test
  delete community all
  if destination in (213.194.95.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy BGP-Customers
  set community BGP-Customers additive
end-policy
!
route-policy ALL_Local_Pref
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any PREF_220 then
    set local-preference 220
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any PREF_150 then
    set local-preference 150
    done
  endif
  #PREF_135
  if community matches-any PREF_135 then
    set local-preference 135
    done
  endif
  #PREF_140
  if community matches-any PREF_140 then
    set local-preference 140
    done
  endif
  #PREF_170
  if community matches-any PREF_170 then
    set local-preference 170
    done
  endif
  #PREF_155
  if community matches-any PREF_155 then
    set local-preference 155
    done
  endif
  #PREF_160
  if community matches-any PREF_160 then
    set local-preference 160
    done
  endif
  #PREF_159
  if community matches-any PREF_159 then
    set local-preference 159
    done
  endif
  #PREF_100
  if community matches-any PREF_100 then
    set local-preference 100
    done
  endif
  set local-preference 200
end-policy

  if community matches-any ROUTE-KES then
    drop
  endif
  done
end-policy

  endif
  drop

!
route-policy RETN-BGP-IMPORT
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  #TEST_ZULA
  if destination in (95.91.246.0/23) then
    drop
  endif
  #Google_DNS_Prefixes
  if destination in Google_DNS_Prefixes then
    set local-preference 130
    set med 5000
    set community DO-NOT-ANNOUNCE-TNAP additive
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    done
  endif
  if as-path in GAME_Server_24940 then
    set local-preference 130
    set community RETN_Esenyurt additive
    done
  endif
  #Seabone_Problem
  if destination in (185.125.231.0/24, 208.184.0.0/15, 46.148.192.0/20, 152.207.0.0/17) then
    set local-preference 130
    set community RETN_Esenyurt additive
    done
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    set local-preference 130
    set community RETN_Esenyurt additive
    done
  endif
  #P3_MICROSOFT_OZEL
  if as-path in MICROSOFT_OZEL then
    set local-preference 130
    set community RETN_Esenyurt additive
    done
  endif
  #P3_FACEBOOK_OZEL
  if as-path in FACEBOOK_OZEL then
    set local-preference 130
    set community RETN_Esenyurt additive
    done
  endif
  #INSTAGRAM_VCNO_ESENTEPEProblem
  if destination in INSTAGRAM_OZEL then
    set local-preference 130
    set community RETN_Esenyurt additive
    done
  endif
  #P3_YOUTUBE_OZEL
  if as-path in YOUTUBE_OZEL then
    set local-preference 130
    set community RETN_Esenyurt additive
    done
  endif
  #P3_WHATSAPP_OZEL
  if as-path in WHATSAPP_OZEL then

  if destination in VF-ipv6-deny-44 then
    drop
  endif
  #BLACKHOLE

    set community VCNO-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community SEABONE-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community INTEROUTE-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community TT-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community LUMEN-BLACKHOLE additive
    done
  endif
  #VF TUZLA PREFIXES
  if community matches-any Customers then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

  #REJECT BOGONS_V6
  if destination in BOGONS_V6 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/48
  if destination in Smaller_than_48 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_LONG_AS_PATH
  if as-path length ge 50 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT INVALID RPKI
  if validation-state is invalid then
    drop
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ################################
  if destination in (2a03:2880:f10c::/48) then
    set local-preference 148
    set community Interoute additive
    set community IPT_COMM additive
    done
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_END ################################
  #DEFAULT
  if destination in ipv6_def then
    set local-preference 130
    set community Interoute additive
    set community IPT_COMM additive
    done
  endif
  set local-preference 130
  set community Interoute additive
  set community IPT_COMM additive
end-policy

  drop
end-policy

route-policy Qwilt_Cache_CDN_Export
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any DO-NOT-ANNOUNCE-TNAP then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT COGENT IP TRANSIT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^174_') then
    drop
  endif
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^3356_') then
    drop
  endif
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^6762_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^9121_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT INTEROUTE PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^8928_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT Superonline PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^34984_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT VCNO IP TRANSIT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^1273_') then
    drop
  endif
  #TNAP REJECT
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^$') then
    drop
  endif
  #Qwilt prefixes
  if community matches-any Qwilt_istanbul_primary or community matches-any Qwilt_izmir_primary or community matches-any Qwilt_istanbul_secondary or community matches-any Qwilt_izmir_secondary then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

!
route-policy ibgp_export_inet_to_rr
  #REJECT RFC1918
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any TT-BLACKHOLE then
    drop
  endif
  #ACCEPT IR PREFIXES
  if community matches-any INTEROUTE then
    done
  endif
  #ACCEPT TNAP PREFIXES
  if community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT TR VOICE BACKBONE FOR EUROPE REDUNDANCY
  if destination in TR_VOICE_BACKBONE then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy to_radore_tier1_export
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any DO-NOT-ANNOUNCE-TNAP then
    drop
  endif
  #Only Announce TC Peering
  if community matches-any TC-Only then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #NETFACTOR-ANNOUNCE-REJECT
  if destination in NETFACTOR-ANNOUNCE-REJECT-radore then
    drop
  endif
  #IP SLA ANONS ET
  if destination in (31.145.124.0/24, 31.145.162.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #IP SLA ANONS KES
  if destination in IPSLA_PREFIXES then
    drop
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Prefixes
  if community matches-any From_VF_to_TNAP then
    done
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Undesired_announce_reject
  if community matches-any From_VF_to_IR or community matches-any From_VF_to_Local then
    drop
  endif
  #Terramark_Kes
  if community matches-any Terramark then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any International-Pops then
    drop
  endif
  #Network-Statements
  if community matches-any Bgp-Main-Network-Statements then
    done
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Bgp-Customers
  if community matches-any Customers then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #Announce-to-Tnap
  if community matches-any Tnap_out then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_allocations
  if community matches-any allocations then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #blackhole
  if community matches-any blackhole then
    done
  endif
  #yurtici_blackhole
  if community matches-any TTNET-Sadece-yurtici then
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_primary
  if community matches-any announce_from_esentepe_atm then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_backup
  if community matches-any announce_from_esentepe_me or community matches-any announce_from_bostanci then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

  #INCITY BNG IPv6_STATIC_NON-CGNAT_ISG_PREFIX
  if destination in INCITY_BNG_IPv6_STATIC_NON-CGNAT then
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    set local-preference 200
    set community VFNET_TT additive
    set community TTNET-Sadece-yurtici additive
    set community Qwilt_istanbul_primary additive
    set community Qwilt_izmir_secondary additive
    set community 8928:15021 additive
    set community 1273:15912 additive
    set community TT_PRIMARY_ESENTEPE_INT2_COMMUNITY_SECONDARY additive
    set community TT_PRIMARY_IZMIR_INT_COMMUNITY_PRIMARY additive
    done
  endif
  #MERSIN _ISG_PREFIX
  if destination in Mersin-IPv6-Isg-PREFIXES then
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    set local-preference 200
    set community VFNET_MERSINISG additive
    set community VFNET_TT additive
    set community TTNET-Sadece-yurtici additive
    set community Qwilt_izmir_primary additive
    set community Qwilt_istanbul_secondary additive
    set community 8928:15021 additive
    set community 1273:15912 additive
    set community TT_PRIMARY_ESENTEPE_INT2_COMMUNITY_SECONDARY additive
    set community TT_PRIMARY_IZMIR_INT_COMMUNITY_PRIMARY additive
    set community SOL_PRIMARY_TUZLA_INT_COMMUNITY_PRIMARY additive
    set community SOL_PRIMARY_IZMIR_INT_COMMUNITY_SECONDARY additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

    set community VFNET_ERZURUMISG additive

    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy Default_and_AS15924_Export
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0) then
    done
  endif
  #Reject-Smaller-Than-/24#
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0 ge 25) then
    drop
  endif
  #remove_rfc1918#
  if destination in (10.0.0.0/8 ge 32, 172.16.0.0/12 ge 32, 192.168.0.0/16 ge 32) then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term#
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks#
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Bgp-Customers#
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    done
  endif
  if as-path in VATHAS_BGP_Customers then
    done
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  if as-path originates-from '15924'  then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy IC-VFNET-CAMLICAISG-IMPORT
  if destination in VFNET-CAMLICAISG-PREFIXES then
    set community VFNET-CAMLICAISG additive
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    set local-preference 200
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

!
route-policy PNI_ESY1_TURKNET_EXPORT_V4
  #REJECT BOGONS_V4
  if destination in BOGONS_V4 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_LONG_AS_PATH
  if as-path length ge 50 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT DEFAULT
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT OLD IPT/PNI COMM 
  if community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT IPT COMM
  if community matches-any IPT_COMM then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT PNI COMM
  if community matches-any PNI_COMM then
    drop
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ###########################################
  #MOBILE FULL
  if as-path in ASN_MOBILE then
    done
  endif
  #FIX FULL
  if as-path in ASN_FIX then
    done
  endif
  #LOCAL FULL
  if as-path in ASN_LOCAL then
    done
  endif
  #CUSTOMERS 
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    done
  endif
  ################################  EXCEPTIONS_END  ###########################################
  #REJECT OTHERS
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy PNI_ESY1_TURKNET_EXPORT_V6
  #REJECT BOGONS_V6
  if destination in BOGONS_V6 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/48
  if destination in Smaller_than_48 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_LONG_AS_PATH
  if as-path length ge 50 then
    drop
  endif
  #TEST
  if destination in (2a00:1880:a000::/42, 2a00:1880:a040::/42, 2a00:1880:a080::/42) then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT INVALID RPKI
  if validation-state is invalid then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT DEFAULT
  if destination in ipv6_def then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT OLD IPT/PNI COMM 
  if community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT IPT COMM
  if community matches-any IPT_COMM then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT PNI COMM
  if community matches-any PNI_COMM then
    drop
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ###########################################
  #MOBILE FULL
  if as-path in ASN_MOBILE then
    done
  endif
  #FIX FULL
  if as-path in ASN_FIX then
    done
  endif
  #LOCAL FULL
  if as-path in ASN_LOCAL then
    done
  endif
  #CUSTOMERS 
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    done
  endif
  ################################  EXCEPTIONS_END  ###########################################
  #REJECT OTHERS
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy PNI_ESY1_TURKNET_IMPORT_V4
  #REJECT BOGONS_V4
  if destination in BOGONS_V4 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_LONG_AS_PATH
  if as-path length ge 50 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT INVALID RPKI
  if validation-state is invalid then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT DEFAULT
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ###########################################
  #ACCEPT ROUTES BY AS-PATH&PREFIXES
  if destination in PNI_ESY1_TURKNET_PREFIXES_V4 and as-path in ASN_TURKNET then
    set local-preference 170
    set community PNI_TURKNET_COMM additive
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community PNI_COMM additive
    done
  endif
  ################################  EXCEPTIONS_END  ###########################################
  #REJECT OTHERS
  drop
end-policy

    drop

    set community Customer-Voice-Subnetted additive
  endif

    set next-hop self
    done
  endif

    done
  endif

    done
  endif
  if community matches-any Level3_Esenyurt then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VCNO_ESENYURT then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any Interoute then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

  drop
end-policy

  if validation-state is invalid then
    drop
  endif

    set local-preference 200
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community KAOPU-ESENYURT additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy ibgp_export_to_m40e2_inet_to_rr
  #TOC SW MANAGEMENT
  if destination in (10.135.198.232/29, 213.161.147.0/24, 176.235.122.0/24, 10.135.201.216/29) then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT RFC1918
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any TT-BLACKHOLE then
    drop
  endif
  #ISG_SOL_RR_Deny
  if community matches-any ISG_SOL_RR_Deny then
    drop
  endif
  #ACCEPT IR Default
  if community matches-any INTEROUTE and destination in Default then
    done
  endif
  #ACCEPT LEVEL3 Default
  if community matches-any Level3_Esenyurt and destination in Default then
    done
  endif
  #ACCEPT VCNO Default
  if community matches-any VCNO_ESENYURT and destination in Default then
    done
  endif
  #ACCEPT TNAP PREFIXES
  if community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT TR VOICE BACKBONE FOR EUROPE REDUNDANCY
  if destination in TR_VOICE_BACKBONE then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

!
route-policy Medianova_Mednautilus_BGP_Export
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  # VFNET_ERLAB
  if destination in (212.15.16.0/20) then
    done
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Prefixes
  if community matches-any ANK_BOLGE_BGP_CUSTOMERS or community matches-any IST_AND_BGP_CUSTOMERS then
    done
  endif
  # VFNET_DSL_INJECTION
  if destination in (81.8.82.0/24, 95.65.252.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #SPESIFIK_ANONS_TO_SOL
  if destination in (82.150.93.0/24) then
    prepend as-path 15924 3
    done
  endif
  # VFNET-Anons-Spesifik
  if community matches-any VFNET-CAMLICA or community matches-any VFNet-Koza and destination in (193.243.192.0/19, 213.194.110.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #ofis_ipleri
  if destination in (213.194.95.0/24, 31.145.9.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #Reject-Term
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  #International-Pops
  if community matches-any International-Pops then
    drop
  endif
  #Network-Statements

route-policy Vodafone_CloudFlare_DENEME_BGP_Export
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^9121_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TURKCELL PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^34984_') then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term-TC-Only
  if community matches-any TC-Only then
    drop
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Prefixes
  if community matches-any ANK_BOLGE_BGP_CUSTOMERS or community matches-any IST_AND_BGP_CUSTOMERS then
    done
  endif
  #BROADBAND_OZEL
  if as-path in BROADBAND then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in (46.221.0.0/18, 31.145.100.0/23) then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    delete community all
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  drop
end-policy

!
route-policy Vodafone_Origin_For_Akamai_BGP_Export
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #For Akamai_Load_Balance
  if destination in (212.65.128.0/19, 193.243.222.120/29, 31.145.57.192/28) then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term-TC-Only
  if community matches-any TC-Only then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any VF-ESY-GGSN or community matches-any VF-TZL-GGSN or community matches-any VF-TZL-Catch_All or community matches-any VF-ESY-GGSN-GR1 or community matches-any VF-ESY-GGSN-GR2 or community matches-any VF-ESY-Catch_All then
    drop
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Prefixes
  if community matches-any ANK_BOLGE_BGP_CUSTOMERS or community matches-any IST_AND_BGP_CUSTOMERS then
    done
  endif
  if destination in (212.65.128.0/19, 193.243.192.0/19, 31.145.0.0/16) then
    done
  endif
  # VFNET_DSL_INJECTION
  if destination in (81.8.82.0/24, 95.65.252.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #ofis_ipleri
  if destination in (213.194.95.0/24, 31.145.9.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #Reject-Term
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  #International-Pops
  if community matches-any International-Pops then
    drop
  endif
  #Network-Statements
  if community matches-any Bgp-Main-Network-Statements then
    done
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    done
  endif
